Source Code

These source-code files were transcribed from scans made from Don Eyles's personal copy of Luminary 069. They were scanned at archive.org's Boston facility, and the scanning was sponsored by Onno Hommes. The code was transcribed from these scans by a team of volunteers who are referenced in the program comments. Comments from the original source code are prefixed with a single '#' symbol, whereas comments added later are prefixed by "##" or "###". In some cases, where similar code blocks exist in previously-transcribed AGC programs (primarily Luminary 99, from Apollo 11) those code blocks were used as a starting point and then corrected to agree with the Luminary 69 scans. The full scans are available at the Virtual AGC project's collection at archive.org, while more-convenient reduced-size (but reduced-quality) images are available at the main Virtual AGC website. Report any errors noted by creating an issue report at the Virtual AGC project's GitHub repository. Notations on the program listing read, in part:

	GAP:  ASSEMBLE REVISION 069 OF AGC PROGRAM LUMINARY BY NASA 2021112-011
	19:02 NOV. 25,1968
Note that the date is the date of the printout, not the date of the program revision. 

022224,000002:                                                                                                  ## Copyright:   Public domain.
022225,000003:                                                                                                  ## Filename:    P20-P25.agc
022226,000004:                                                                                                  ## Purpose:     The main source file for Luminary revision 069.
022227,000005:                                                                                                  ##              It is part of the source code for the original release
022228,000006:                                                                                                  ##              of the flight software for the Lunar Module's (LM) Apollo
022229,000007:                                                                                                  ##              Guidance Computer (AGC) for Apollo 10. The actual flown
022230,000008:                                                                                                  ##              version was Luminary 69 revision 2, which included a
022231,000009:                                                                                                  ##              newer lunar gravity model and only affected module 2.
022232,000010:                                                                                                  ##              This file is intended to be a faithful transcription, except
022233,000011:                                                                                                  ##              that the code format has been changed to conform to the
022234,000012:                                                                                                  ##              requirements of the yaYUL assembler rather than the
022235,000013:                                                                                                  ##              original YUL assembler.
022236,000014:                                                                                                  ## Reference:   pp. 504-623
022237,000015:                                                                                                  ## Assembler:   yaYUL
022238,000016:                                                                                                  ## Contact:     Ron Burkey <info@sandroid.org>.
022239,000017:                                                                                                  ## Website:     www.ibiblio.org/apollo/index.html
022240,000018:                                                                                                  ## Mod history: 2016-12-13 MAS  Created from Luminary 99.
022241,000019:                                                                                                  ##              2016-12-14 MAS  Updated from comment-proofed Luminary 99 version.
022242,000020:                                                                                                  ##              2016-01-16 HG   Transcribed
022243,000021:                                                                                                  ##              2017-01-22 HG   Shift pseudo label +3 to column 2.
022244,000022:                                                                                                  ##                              Add missing operator INHINT
022245,000023:                                                                                                  ##              2017-01-23 HG   Fix operator CCS -> CA
022246,000024:                                                                                                  ##                              Fix value TENDEG .27... -> .027...
022247,000025:                                                                                                  ##                              Fix operand R22LEM42 -> R22LEM
022248,000026:                                                                                                  ##                                          GOXDSPF  -> GOXDSPFR
022249,000027:                                                                                                  ##                                          BIT13    -> BIT3
022250,000028:                                                                                                  ##                              Fix operand modifier WWPOS +6 -> WWPOS +4
022251,000029:                                                                                                  ##                              Fix statement CA FLAGWRD2 -> CS FLAGWRD0
022252,000030:                                                                                                  ##                                            EXTEND      -> CCS A
022253,000031:                                                                                                  ##                                            BZF NOTP20  -> TC  NOTP20
022254,000032:                                                                                                  ##              2017-01-27 RSB  Proofed comment text using octopus/prooferComments
022255,000033:                                                                                                  ##                              and fixed errors found.
022256,000034:                                                                                                  ##              2017-01-28 RSB  WTIH -> WITH.
022257,000035: 
022258,000036:                                                                                                  ##

022260,000038: 
022261,000039:                                                                                                  #  RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION PROGRAM 20
022262,000040:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
022263,000041:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 2
022264,000042:                                                                                                  #  BY  P. VOLANTE
022265,000043:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
022266,000044: 
022267,000045:                                                                                                  #    THE PURPOSE OF THIS PROGRAM IS TO CONTROL THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR FROM
022268,000046:                                                                                                  #  STARTUP THROUGH ACQUISITION AND LOCKON TO THE CSM AND TO UPDATE EITHER
022269,000047:                                                                                                  #  THE LM OR CSM STATE VECTOR (AS SPECIFIED BY THE ASTRONAUT BY DSKY ENTRY)
022270,000048:                                                                                                  #  ON THE BASIS OF THE RR TRACKING DATA.
022271,000049:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
022272,000050: 
022273,000051:                                                                                                  #  ASTRONAUT REQUEST THROUGH DSKY V37E20E
022274,000052:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
022275,000053:                                                                                                  #    R02BOTH (IMU STATUS CHECK)               FLAGUP
022276,000054:                                                                                                  #    GOFLASH (PINBALL-DISPLAY)                FLAGDOWN
022277,000055:                                                                                                  #    R23LEM  (MANUAL ACQUISITION)             BANKCALL
022278,000056:                                                                                                  #    LS201   (LOS DETERMINATION)              TASKOVER
022279,000057:                                                                                                  #    LS202   (RANGE LIMIT TEST)
022280,000058:                                                                                                  #    R61LEM  (PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE)
022281,000059:                                                                                                  #    R21LEM  (RR DESIGNATE)                   ENDOFJOB
022282,000060:                                                                                                  #    R22LEM  (DATA READ)                      GOPERF1
022283,000061:                                                                                                  #    R31LEM  (RENDEZVOUS PARAMETER DISPLAY)
022284,000062:                                                                                                  #    PRIOLARM (PRIORITY DISPLAY)
022285,000063:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES-
022286,000064:                                                                                                  #    P20 MAY BE TERMINATED IN TWO WAYS-ASTRONAUT SELECTION OF IDLING
022287,000065:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM (P00) BY KEYING V37E00E OR BY KEYING IN V56E
022288,000066:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES-
022289,000067:                                                                                                  #    RANGE GREATER THAN 400 NM DISPLAY
022290,000068:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
022291,000069:                                                                                                  #    TRKMKCNT = NO OF RENDEZVOUS TRACKING MARKS TAKEN (COUNTER)
022292,000070:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
022293,000071:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
022294,000072:                                                                                                  #    SRCHOPT,RNDVZFLG,ACMODFLG,VEHUPFLG,UPDATFLG,TRACKFLG,
022295,000073:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
022296,000074:                                                                                                  #    CENTRALS-A,Q,L
022297,000075: 25,2062  30,2000                                  SBANK=   LOWSUPER                              #  FOR LOW 2CADR'S.
022298,000076: 
022299,000077: 33,2045                                           BANK     33                                    
022300,000078: 24,2000                                           SETLOC   P20S                                  
022301,000079: 24,2000                                           BANK                                           
022302,000080: 
022303,000081: 24,2022  E7,1454                                  EBANK=   LOSCOUNT                              
022304,000082: 24,2022                                           COUNT*   $$/P20                                
022305,000083: 24,2022  24,2022               PROG22             =        PROG20

022734,000512:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
022735,000513:                                                                                                  #  PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE PROGRAM P25
022736,000514:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 3
022737,000515:                                                                                                  #  BY  P. VOLANTE
022738,000516:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
022739,000517: 
022740,000518:                                                                                                  #    THE PURPOSE OF THIS PROGRAM IS TO COMPUTE THE PREFERRED TRACKING
022741,000519:                                                                                                  #  ATTITUDE OF THE LM TO CONTINUOUSLY POINT THE LM TRACKING BEACON AT THE
022742,000520:                                                                                                  #  CSM AND TO PERFORM THE MANEUVER TO THE PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE AND
022743,000521:                                                                                                  #  CONTINUOUSLY MAINTAIN THIS ATTITUDE WITHIN PRESCRIBED LIMITS
022744,000522:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
022745,000523:                                                                                                  #    ASTRONAUT REQUEST THROUGH DSKY V37E25E
022746,000524:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED -
022747,000525:                                                                                                  #    BANKCALL                      FLAGUP
022748,000526:                                                                                                  #    R02BOTH  (IMU STATUS CHECK)   ENDOFJOB
022749,000527:                                                                                                  #    R61LEM   (PREF TRK ATT ROUT)  WAITLIST
022750,000528:                                                                                                  #    TASKOVER                      FINDVAC
022751,000529:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES  -
022752,000530:                                                                                                  #    P25 MAY BE TERMINATED IN TWO WAYS-ASTRONAUT SELECTION OF IDLING
022753,000531:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM(P00) BY KEYING V37E00E OR BY KEYING IN V56E
022754,000532:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
022755,000533:                                                                                                  #    NONE
022756,000534:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
022757,000535:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
022758,000536:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
022759,000537:                                                                                                  #    TRACKFLG,P25FLAG
022760,000538:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
022761,000539:                                                                                                  #    NONE
022762,000540: 24,2427  E7,1454                                  EBANK=   LOSCOUNT

022809,000587:                                                                                                  #  DATA READ ROUTINE 22 (LEM)
022810,000588:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
022811,000589:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 2
022812,000590:                                                                                                  #  BY P VOLANTE
022813,000591:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
022814,000592: 
022815,000593:                                                                                                  #    TO PROCESS AUTOMATIC RR MARK DATA TO UPDATE THE STATE VECTOR OF EITHER
022816,000594:                                                                                                  #  LM OR CSM AS DEFINED IN THE RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION PROGRAM (P20)
022817,000595:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
022818,000596:                                                                                                  #           TC     BANKCALL
022819,000597:                                                                                                  #           CADR   R22LEM
022820,000598:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED -
022821,000599:                                                                                                  #    LSR22.1           GOFLASH        WAITLIST
022822,000600:                                                                                                  #    LSR22.2           PRIOLARM       BANKCALL
022823,000601:                                                                                                  #    LSR22.3           R61LEM
022824,000602:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES-
022825,000603:                                                                                                  #    R22 WILL CONTINUE TO RECYCLE,UPDATING STATE VECTORS WITH RADAR DATA
022826,000604:                                                                                                  #  UNTIL P20 CEASES TO OPERATE (RENDEZVOUS FLAG SET TO ZERO) AT WHICH TIME
022827,000605:                                                                                                  #  R22 WILL TERMINATE SELF.
022828,000606:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES-
022829,000607:                                                                                                  #    PRIORITY ALARM

023010,000788:                                                                                                  #  RR DESIGNATE ROUTINE (R21LEM)
023011,000789:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
023012,000790:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 2
023013,000791:                                                                                                  #  BY P VOLANTE
023014,000792:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
023015,000793: 
023016,000794:                                                                                                  #    TO POINT THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR AT THE CSM UNTIL AUTOMATIC ACQUISITION
023017,000795:                                                                                                  #  OF THE CSM IS ACCOMPLISHED BY THE RADAR. ROUTINE IS CALLED BY P20.
023018,000796:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
023019,000797:                                                                                                  #           TC     BANKCALL
023020,000798:                                                                                                  #           CADR   R21LEM
023021,000799:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED -
023022,000800:                                                                                                  #    FINDVAC        FLAGUP           ENDOFJOB        PRIOLARM
023023,000801:                                                                                                  #    NOVAC          INTPRET          LPS20.1         PHASCHNG
023024,000802:                                                                                                  #    WAITLIST       JOBSLEEP         JOBWAKE         FLAGDOWN
023025,000803:                                                                                                  #    TASKOVER       BANKCALL         RADSTALL        RRDESSM
023026,000804:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES
023027,000805:                                                                                                  #    WHEN LOCK-ON IS ACHIEVED,BRANCH WILL BE TO P20 WHERE R22 (DATA READ
023028,000806:                                                                                                  #  WILL BE SELECTED OR A NEED FOR A MANEUVER(BRANCH TO P20LEMA)
023029,000807:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES-
023030,000808:                                                                                                  #    PRIORITY ALARM 503 WHEN LOCK-ON HASN:T BEEN ACHIEVED AFTER 30SECS -
023031,000809:                                                                                                  #  THIS REQUIRES ASTRONAUT INTERFACE- SELECTION OF SEARCH OPTION OF
023032,000810:                                                                                                  #  ACQUISITION
023033,000811:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
023034,000812:                                                                                                  #    SEE LPS20.1,RRDESSM
023035,000813:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
023036,000814:                                                                                                  #    RRTARGET,RADMODES ARE USED BY LPS20.1 AND RRDESSM
023037,000815:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
023038,000816:                                                                                                  #    LOSCMFLG      LOKONSW
023039,000817:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
023040,000818:                                                                                                  #    SEE LPS20.1,RRDESSM
023041,000819: 24,2721  E7,1454                                  EBANK=   LOSCOUNT                              
023042,000820: 24,2721                                           COUNT*   $$/R21                                
023043,000821: 24,2721           32341        R21LEM             CAF      MAXTRIES                              #  ALLOW 60 PASSES (APPROX 45 SECS.) TO
023044,000822: 24,2722           55114                           TS       DESCOUNT                              #  DESIGNATE AND LOCKON
023045,000823: 24,2723           02714                           TC       LUNSFCHK                              
023046,000824: 24,2724           02731                           TC       R21LEM5                               
023047,000825: 24,2725           34755                           CAF      ZERO                                  #       COMMAND ANTENNA TO MODE CENTER

023191,000969:                                                                                                  #  SEARCH ROUTINE R24LEM
023192,000970:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
023193,000971:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 2
023194,000972:                                                                                                  #  BY  P. VOLANTE
023195,000973:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
023196,000974: 
023197,000975:                                                                                                  #    TO ACQUIRE THE CSM BY A SEARCH PATTERN WHEN THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR HAS
023198,000976:                                                                                                  #  FAILED TO ACQUIRE THE CSM IN THE AUTOMATIC TRACKING MODE AND TO ALLOW
023199,000977:                                                                                                  #  THE ASTRONAUT TO CONFIRM THAT REACQUISITION HAS NOT BEEN BY SIDELOBE.
023200,000978:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE
023201,000979:                                                                                                  #           CAF    PRIONN
023202,000980:                                                                                                  #           TC     FINDVAC
023203,000981:                                                                                                  #           EBANK= DATAGOOD
023204,000982:                                                                                                  #           2CADR  R24LEM
023205,000983:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
023206,000984:                                                                                                  #    FLAGUP        FLAGDOWN      BANKCALL
023207,000985:                                                                                                  #    R61LEM        GOFLASHR      FINDVAC
023208,000986:                                                                                                  #    ENDOFJOB      NOVAC         LSR24.1
023209,000987:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES-
023210,000988:                                                                                                  #    ASTRONAUT RESPONSE TO DISPLAY OF OMEGA AND DATAGOOD.HE CAN EITHER
023211,000989:                                                                                                  #  REJECT BY TERMINATING (SEARCH OPTION AND RESELECTING P20) OR ACCEPT BY
023212,000990:                                                                                                  #  PROCEEDING (EXIT ROUTINE AND RETURN TO AUTO MODE IN P20)
023213,000991:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES-
023214,000992:                                                                                                  #    SEE NORMAL EXIT MODES ABOVE
023215,000993:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT -
023216,000994:                                                                                                  #    SEE OUTPUT FROM LSR24.1 + R61LEM
023217,000995:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
023218,000996:                                                                                                  #    SEE INPUT FOR LSR24.1
023219,000997:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
023220,000998:                                                                                                  #    SRCHOPT,ACMODFLG
023221,000999: 24,3100  E7,1731                                  EBANK=   DATAGOOD                              
023222,001000: 24,3100                                           COUNT*   $$/R24                                
023223,001001: 24,3100           05504        R24LEM             TC       UPFLAG

023225,001003: 24,3102           05516                           TC       DOWNFLAG                              #  RESET LOS BEING COMPUTED FLAG TO MAKE
023226,001004: 24,3103           00041                           ADRES    LOSCMFLG                              #  SURE DODES DOESN'T GO TO R21
023227,001005: 24,3104           34755        R24LEM1            CAF      ZERO

023488,001266:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRLIMCHK                                                  ARE IN THE LIMITS OF THE CURRENT MODE.
023489,001267: 
023490,001268:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023491,001269:                                                                                                  #  RRLIMCHK CHECKS RR DESIRED GIMBAL ANGLES TO SEE IF THEY ARE WITHIN
023492,001270:                                                                                                  #  THE LIMITS OF THE CURRENT MODE. INITIALLY THE DESIRED TRUNNION AND
023493,001271:                                                                                                  #  SHAFT ANGLES ARE STORED IN ITEMP1 AND ITEMP2. THE CURRENT RR
023494,001272:                                                                                                  #  ANTENNAE MODE (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED WHICH IS = 0 FOR
023495,001273:                                                                                                  #  MODE 1 AND =1 FOR MODE 2.
023496,001274:                                                                                                  #  MODE 1 - THE TRUNNION ANGLE IS CHECKED AT MAGSUB TO SEE IF IT IS
023497,001275:                                                                                                  #  BETWEEN -55 AND +55 DEGREES. IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2. IF WITHIN LIMITS,
023498,001276:                                                                                                  #  THE SHAFT ANGLE IS CHECKED TO SEE IF IT IS BETWEEN -70 AND +59 DEGREES.
023499,001277:                                                                                                  #  IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2. IF IN LIMITS, RETURN TO L +3.
023500,001278:                                                                                                  #  MODE 2 - THE SHAFT ANGLE IS CHECKED AT MAGSUB TO SEE IF IT IS
023501,001279:                                                                                                  #  BETWEEN -139 AND -25 DEGREES. IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2. IF WITHIN
023502,001280:                                                                                                  #  LIMITS, THE TRUNNION ANGLE IS CHECKED TO SEE IF IT IS BETWEEN +125
023503,001281:                                                                                                  #  AND -125 (+235) DEGREES. IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2. IF IN LIMITS, RETURN
023504,001282:                                                                                                  #  TO L +3.
023505,001283: 
023506,001284:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023507,001285:                                                                                                  #  L  TC  RRLIMCHK (WITH INTERRUPT INHIBITED)
023508,001286:                                                                                                  #  L +1  ADRES  T,S  (DESIRED TRUNNION ANGLE ADDRESS)
023509,001287: 
023510,001288:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023511,001289:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES, MODEA, MODEB (OR DESIRED TRUNNION AND SHAFT
023512,001290:                                                                                                  #  ANGLES ELSEWHERE IN CONSECUTIVE LOCATIONS - UNSWITCHED ERASABLE OR
023513,001291:                                                                                                  #  CURRENT EBANK).
023514,001292:

023516,001294:

023568,001346:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  SETTRKF                                                  . IF EITHER:
023569,001347: 
023570,001348:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023571,001349:                                                                                                  #  SETTRKF UPDATES THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP ON THE DSKY.                      HER THE ALT OR VEL INFORMATION.
023572,001350:                                                                                                  #  INITIALLY THE LAMP TEST FLAG (IMODES33 BIT 1) IS CHECKED.
023573,001351:                                                                                                  #  IF A LAMP TEST IS IN PROGRESS, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L +1.
023574,001352:                                                                                                  #  IF NO LAMP TEST THE FOLLOWING IS CHECKED SEQUENTIALLY_
023575,001353:                                                                                                  #  1) RR CDU:S BEING ZEROED, RR CDU OK, AND RR NOT IN
023576,001354:                                                                                                  #  AUTO MODE (RADMODES BITS 13, 7, 2).
023577,001355:                                                                                                  #  2) LR VEL DATA FAIL AND NO LR POS DATA (RADMODES BITS
023578,001356:                                                                                                  #  8,5)
023579,001357:                                                                                                  #  3) NO RR DATA (RADMODES BIT 4)
023580,001358:                                                                                                  #  THE ABSENCE OF ALL THREE SIMULTANEOUSLY IN (1), THE PRESENCE OF BOTH
023581,001359:                                                                                                  #  IN (2), AND THE PRESENCE OF (3) RESULTS IN EITHER THE TRACKER FAIL
023582,001360:                                                                                                  #  LAMP (DSPTAB +11D BIT 8) BEING TURNED ON OR LEFT ON. OTHERWISE,
023583,001361:                                                                                                  #  THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP IS TURNED OFF OR IS LEFT OFF. THEREFORE, THE
023584,001362:                                                                                                  #  TRACKER FAIL LAMP IS TURNED ON IF_
023585,001363:                                                                                                  #  A ) RR CDU FAILED WITH RR IN AUTO MODE AND RR CDU:S NOT BEING ZEROED.
023586,001364:                                                                                                  #  B) N SAMPLES OF LR DATA COULD NOT BE TAKEN IN 2N TRIES WITH
023587,001365:                                                                                                  #  EITHER THE ALT OR VEL INFORMATION
023588,001366:                                                                                                  #  C) N SAMPLES OF RR DATA COULD NOT BE OBTAINED FROM 2N TRIES
023589,001367:                                                                                                  #  WITH EITHER THE AL
023590,001368:

023639,001417:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRTURNON
023640,001418: 
023641,001419:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023642,001420: 
023643,001421:                                                                                                  #  RRTURNON IS THE TURN-ON SEQUENCE WHICH, ALONG WITH
023644,001422:                                                                                                  #  RRZEROSB, ZEROS THE CDU:S AND DETERMINES THE RR MODE.
023645,001423:                                                                                                  #  INITIALLY, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO RRZEROSB FOR THE
023646,001424:                                                                                                  #  ACTUAL TURN-ON SEQUENCE. UPON RETURN THE PROGRAM
023647,001425:                                                                                                  #  WAITS 1 SECOND BEFORE REMOVING THE TURN-ON FLAG
023648,001426:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT1) SO THE REPOSITION ROUTINE WON:T
023649,001427:                                                                                                  #  INITIATE PROGRAM ALARM 00501. A CHECK IS THEN MADE
023650,001428:                                                                                                  #  TO SEE IF A PROGRAM IS USING THE RR (STATE BIT 7). IF
023651,001429:                                                                                                  #  SO, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO ENDRADAR SO THAT THE RR CDU
023652,001430:                                                                                                  #  FAIL FLAG (RADMODES BIT 7) CAN BE CHECKED BEFORE
023653,001431:                                                                                                  #  RETURNING TO THE WAITING PROGRAM. IF NOT, THE PROGRAM EXITS
023654,001432:                                                                                                  #  TO TASKOVER.
023655,001433: 
023656,001434:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE: WAITLIST TASK FROM RRAUTCHK IF THE RR POWER ON AUTO
023657,001435:                                                                                                  #  BIT (CHAN 33 BIT 2) CHANGES TO 0 AND NO PROGRAM WAS USING
023658,001436:                                                                                                  #  THE RR (STATE BIT 7).
023659,001437: 
023660,001438:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023661,001439:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES, STATE
023662,001440: 
023663,001441:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_  RRZEROSB, FIXDELAY, TASKOVER, ENDRADAR
023664,001442: 
023665,001443:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
023666,001444:                                                                                                  #  NONE
023667,001445: 
023668,001446:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE (SEE RRZEROSB)
023669,001447: 
023670,001448:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  TASKOVER, ENDRADAR (WAITING PROGRAM)
023671,001449: 
023672,001450: 24,3151                                           BANK     24                                    
023673,001451: 25,2000                                           SETLOC   P20S1                                 
023674,001452: 25,2000                                           BANK                                           
023675,001453: 
023676,001454: 25,2062  E7,1454                                  EBANK=   LOSCOUNT                              
023677,001455: 25,2062                                           COUNT*   $$/RSUB                               
023678,001456: 25,2062           02071        RRTURNON           TC       RRZEROSB                              
023679,001457: 25,2063           05221                           TC       FIXDELAY                              #  WAIT 1 SEC BEFORE REMOVING TURN ON FLAG
023680,001458: 25,2064           00144                           DEC      100        B-14                       #  SO A MONITOR REPOSITION WONT ALARM.
023681,001459: 25,2065           44753                           CS       BIT1                                  
023682,001460: 25,2066           70110                           MASK     RADMODES

023687,001465:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRZEROSB
023688,001466: 
023689,001467:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023690,001468:                                                                                                  #  RRZEROSB IS A CLOSED SUBROUTINE TO ZERO THE RR CDU:S,
023691,001469:                                                                                                  #  DETERMINE THE RR MODE, AND TURNS ON THE TRACKER FAIL
023692,001470:                                                                                                  #  LAMP IF REQUIRED. INITIALLY THE RR CDU ZERO BIT (CHAN 12
023693,001471:                                                                                                  #  BIT 1) IS SET. FOLLOWING A 20 MILLISECOND WAIT, THE LGC
023694,001472:                                                                                                  #  RR CDU COUNTERS (OPTY, OPTX) ARE SET = 0 AFTER
023695,001473:                                                                                                  #  WHICH THE RR CDU ZERO DISCRETE (CHAN 12 BIT 1) IS
023696,001474:                                                                                                  #  REMOVED. A 4 SECOND WAIT IS SET TO ALL THE RR CDU:S
023697,001475:                                                                                                  #  TO REPEAT THE ACTUAL TRUNNION AND SHAFT ANGLES. THE
023698,001476:                                                                                                  #  RR CDU ZERO FLAG (RADMODES BIT 13) IS REMOVED. THE
023699,001477:                                                                                                  #  CONTENTS OF OPTY IS THEN CHECKED TO SEE IF THE TRUNNION
023700,001478:                                                                                                  #  ANGLE IS LESS THAN 90 DEGREES. IF NOT, BIT 12 OF
023701,001479:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES IS SET = 1 TO INDICATE RR ANTENNA MODE 2.
023702,001480:                                                                                                  #  IF LESS THAN 90 DEGREES, BIT 12 OF RADMODES IS SET = 0 TO
023703,001481:                                                                                                  #  INDICATE RR ANTENNA MODE 1. SETTRKF IS THEN CALLED TO
023704,001482:                                                                                                  #  SEE IF THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP SHOULD BE TURNED ON.
023705,001483: 
023706,001484:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE: L  TC  RRZEROSB (FROM RRTURNON AND RRZERO)
023707,001485:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023708,001486:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES (BIT 13 SET), DSPTAB +11D
023709,001487: 
023710,001488:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_  FIXDELAY, MAGSUB, SETTRKF
023711,001489: 
023712,001490:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
023713,001491:                                                                                                  #  NONE
023714,001492: 
023715,001493:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  TRACKER FAIL
023716,001494: 
023717,001495:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  L +1 (ALWAYS)
023718,001496: 
023719,001497: 25,2071           00006        RRZEROSB           EXTEND                                         
023720,001498: 25,2072           23315                           QXCH     RRRET                                 
023721,001499: 25,2073           34753                           CAF      BIT1                                  #  BIT 13 OF RADMODES MUST BE SET BEFORE
023722,001500: 25,2074           00006                           EXTEND                                         #  COMING HERE.
023723,001501: 25,2075           05012                           WOR      CHAN12                                #  TURN ON ZERO RR CDU
023724,001502: 25,2076           05221                           TC       FIXDELAY                              
023725,001503: 25,2077           00002                           DEC      2          B-14                       
023726,001504: 
023727,001505: 25,2100           34755                           CAF      ZERO                                  
023728,001506: 25,2101           54035                           TS       CDUT                                  
023729,001507: 25,2102           54036                           TS       CDUS                                  
023730,001508: 25,2103           44753                           CS       ONE                                   #  REMOVE ZEROING BIT.
023731,001509: 25,2104           00006                           EXTEND

023734,001512: 25,2107           01750                           DEC      1000       B-14                       #  RESET FAIL INHIBIT IN 10 SECS - D.281
023735,001513:

023737,001515:

Page 539 

023739,001517: 25,2111           70110                           MASK     RADMODES

023761,001539:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  DORREPOS
023762,001540:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023763,001541:                                                                                                  #  DORREPOS IS A SEQUENCE OF TASKS TO DRIVE THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR
023764,001542:                                                                                                  #  TO A SAFE POSITION. INITIALLY SETRRECR IS CALLED WHERE THE RR
023765,001543:                                                                                                  #  ERROR COUNTERS (CHAN 12 BIT 2) ARE ENABLED AND LASTYCMD
023766,001544:                                                                                                  #  AND LASTXCMD SET = 0 TO INDICATE THE DIFFERENCE BETWEEN THE
023767,001545:                                                                                                  #  DESIRED STATE AND PRESENT STATE OF THE COMMANDS. THE RR
023768,001546:                                                                                                  #  TURN-ON FLAG (RADMODES BIT 1) IS CHECKED AND IF NOT PRESENT,
023769,001547:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM ALARM 00501 IS REQUESTED BEFORE CONTINUING. IN EITHER
023770,001548:                                                                                                  #  CASE, FOLLOWING A 20 MILLISECOND WAIT THE PROGRAM CHECKS THE CURRENT
023771,001549:                                                                                                  #  RR ANTENNA MODE (RADMODES BIT 12). RRTONLY IS THEN CALLED
023772,001550:                                                                                                  #  TO DRIVE THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1 AND TO 180
023773,001551:                                                                                                  #  DEGREES IF IN MODE 2. UPON RETURN, THE CURRENT RR ANTENNA
023774,001552:                                                                                                  #  MODE (RADMODES BIT 12) IS AGAIN CHECKED. RRSONLY IS THEN
023775,001553:                                                                                                  #  CALLED TO DRIVE THE SHAFT ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1 AND TO
023776,001554:                                                                                                  #  -90 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2. IF DURING RRTONLY OR RRSONLY A
023777,001555:                                                                                                  #  REMODE HAS BEEN REQUESTED (RADMODES BIT 14), AND ALWAYS
023778,001556:                                                                                                  #  FOLLOWING COMPLETION OF RRSONLY, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO
023779,001557:                                                                                                  #  REPOSRPT. HERE THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS
023780,001558:                                                                                                  #  REMOVED. A CHECK IS THEN MADE ON THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
023781,001559:                                                                                                  #  BIT 10). IF PRESENT, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO BEGDES. IF NOT PRESENT
023782,001560:                                                                                                  #  INDICATING NO FURTHER ANTENNA CONTROL REQUIRED, THE RR ERROR
023783,001561:                                                                                                  #  COUNTER BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2) IS REMOVED AND THE ROUTINE EXITS TO
023784,001562:                                                                                                  #  TASKOVER.
023785,001563: 
023786,001564:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023787,001565:                                                                                                  #  WAITLIST CALL FROM RRGIMON IF TRUNNION AND SHAFT CDU ANGLES
023788,001566:                                                                                                  #  NOT WITHIN LIMITS OF CURRENT MODE.
023789,001567: 
023790,001568:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023791,001569:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES
023792,001570: 
023793,001571:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
023794,001572:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY, RRSONLY, BEGDES (EXIT)
023795,001573: 
023796,001574:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
023797,001575:                                                                                                  #  NONE
023798,001576: 
023799,001577:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS-  NONE
023800,001578: 
023801,001579:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  TASKOVER, BEGDES
023802,001580:

023850,001628:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  REMODE                                                   IVES SHAFT TO -45, AND FINALLY DRIVES
023851,001629: 
023852,001630:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_                                                 S DONE WITH SINGLE AXIS ROTATIONS (SEE
023853,001631:                                                                                                  #  REMODE IS THE GENERAL REMODING SUBROUTINE. IT DRIVES THE
023854,001632:                                                                                                  #  TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF THE CURRENT MODE IS MODE 1,
023855,001633:                                                                                                  #  180 DEGREES FOR MODE 2, THEN DRIVES THE SHAFT ANGLE TO -45
023856,001634:                                                                                                  #  DEGREES, AND FINALLY DRIVES THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO -130 DEGREES,
023857,001635:                                                                                                  #  TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 2, -50 DEGREES FOR MODE 1, BEFORE
023858,001636:                                                                                                  #  INITIATING 2-AXIS CONTROL. ALL REMODING IS DONE WITH SINGLE
023859,001637:                                                                                                  #  AXIS ROTATIONS (RR1AXIS). INITIALLY THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG
023860,001638:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED. CONTROL IS THEN TRANSFERRED TO
023861,001639:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY TO DRIVE THR TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1
023862,001640:                                                                                                  #  OR 180 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2. RRSONLY IS THEN CALLED TO DRIVE
023863,001641:                                                                                                  #  THE SHAFT ANGLE TO -45 DEGREES. THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG
023864,001642:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED AGAIN. CONTROL IS AGAIN
023865,001643:                                                                                                  #  TRANSFERRED TO RRTONLY TO DRIVE THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO -130
023866,001644:                                                                                                  #  DEGREES TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 2 IF CURRENTLY IN MODE 1 OR TO
023867,001645:                                                                                                  #  -50 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2 TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 1. RMODINV
023868,001646:                                                                                                  #  IS THEN CALLED TO SET RADMODES BIT 12 TO INDICATE THE NEW
023869,001647:                                                                                                  #  RR ANTENNA MODE. THE REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14)
023870,001648:                                                                                                  #  IS REMOVED TO INDICATE THAT REMODING IS COMPLETE. THE PROGRAM
023871,001649:                                                                                                  #  THEN EXITS TO STDESIG TO BEGIN 2-AXIS CONTROL.
023872,001650: 
023873,001651:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023874,001652:                                                                                                  #  FROM BEGDES WHEN REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14) IS SET.
023875,001653:                                                                                                  #  THIS FLAG MAY BE SET IN RRDESSM AND RRDESNB IF RRLIMCHK
023876,001654:                                                                                                  #  DETERMINES THAT THE DESIRED ANGLES ARE WITHIN THE LIMITS OF THE
023877,001655:                                                                                                  #  OTHER MODE.
023878,001656: 
023879,001657:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023880,001658:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES
023881,001659: 
023882,001660:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
023883,001661:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY, RRSONLY, RMODINV (ACTUALLY PART OF)
023884,001662:

023886,001664:                                                                                                  #  NONE

023944,001722:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAMES_  RRTONLY, RRSONLY
023945,001723: 
023946,001724:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023947,001725:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY AND RRSONLY ARE SUBROUTINES FOR DOING SINGLE AXIS
023948,001726:                                                                                                  #  RR MANEUVERS FOR REMODE AND REPOSITION. IT DRIVES TO
023949,001727:                                                                                                  #  WITHIN 1 DEGREE. INITIALLY, AT RR1AX2, THE REMODE AND REPOSITION
023950,001728:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS (RADMODES BITS 14, 11) ARE CHECKED. IF BOTH EXIST,
023951,001729:                                                                                                  #  THE PROGRAM EXITS TO REPOSRPT (SEE DORREPOS). THIS INDICATES
023952,001730:                                                                                                  #  THAT SOMEONE POSSIBLY REQUESTED A DESIGNATE (RADMODES BIT 10)
023953,001731:                                                                                                  #  WHICH REQUIRES A REMODE (RADMODES BIT 14) AND THAT A
023954,001732:                                                                                                  #  REPOSITION IS IN PROGRESS (RADMODES BIT 11). IF NONE
023955,001733:                                                                                                  #  OR ONLY ONE OF THE FLAGS EXIST, REMODE OR REPOSITION, MAGSUB
023956,001734:                                                                                                  #  IS CALLED TO SEE IF THE APPROPRIATE ANGLE IS WITHIN 1 DEGREE. IF YES,
023957,001735:                                                                                                  #  CONTROL RETURNS TO THE CALLING ROUTINE. IF NOT, CONTROL IS
023958,001736:                                                                                                  #  TRANSFERRED TO RROUT FOR SINGLE AXIS MANEUVERS WITH THE OTHER
023959,001737:                                                                                                  #  ANGLE SET = 0. FOLLOWING A .5 SECOND WAIT, THE ABOVE PROCEDURE IS
023960,001738:                                                                                                  #  REPEATED.
023961,001739: 
023962,001740:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE: L-1 CAF *ANGLE* (DESIRED ANGLE SCALED PI)
023963,001741:                                                                                                  #  L  TC  RRTONLY (TRUNNION ONLY)
023964,001742:                                                                                                  #  RRSONLY (SHAFT ONLY)
023965,001743:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY IS CALLED BY PREPOS29;
023966,001744:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY AND RRSONLY ARE CALLED BY DORREPOS AND REMODE
023967,001745: 
023968,001746:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023969,001747:                                                                                                  #  C(A) = DESIRED ANGLE, RADMODES
023970,001748: 
023971,001749:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
023972,001750:                                                                                                  #  FIXDELAY, REPOSRPT, MAGSUB, RROUT
023973,001751: 
023974,001752:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
023975,001753:                                                                                                  #  NONE
023976,001754: 
023977,001755:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
023978,001756: 
023979,001757:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  REPOSRPT (REMODE AND REPOSITION FLAGS PRESENT - RADMODES
023980,001758:                                                                                                  #  BITS 14, 11)
023981,001759:                                                                                                  #  L+1  (ANGLE WITHIN ONE DEGREE OR RR OUT OF AUTO MODE)

024033,001811:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RROUT                                                    RROR COUNTER SCALING. RROUT LIMITS THEM
024034,001812: 
024035,001813:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
024036,001814:                                                                                                  #  RROUT RECEIVES RR GYRO COMMANDS IN TANG, TANG +1 IN RR
024037,001815:                                                                                                  #  ERROR COUNTER SCALING. RROUT THEN LIMITS THEM AND
024038,001816:                                                                                                  #  GENERATES COMMANDS TO THE CDU TO ADJUST THE ERROR COUNTERS
024039,001817:                                                                                                  #  TO THE DESIRED VALUES. INITIALLY MAGSUB CHECKS THE MAGNITUDE OF
024040,001818:                                                                                                  #  THE COMMAND (SHAFT ON 1ST PASS) TO SEE IF IT IS GREATER THAN
024041,001819:                                                                                                  #  384 PULSES. IF NOT, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO RROUTLIM TO
024042,001820:                                                                                                  #  LIMIT THE COMMAND TO +384 OR -384 PULSES. THE DIFFERENCE IS
024043,001821:                                                                                                  #  THEN CALCULATED BETWEEN THE DESIRED STATE AND THE PRESENT STATE OF
024044,001822:                                                                                                  #  THE ERROR COUNTER AS RECORDED IN LASTYCMD AND LASTXCMD.
024045,001823:                                                                                                  #  THE RESULT IS STORED IN OPTXCMD (1ST PASS) AND OPTYCMD (2ND
024046,001824:                                                                                                  #  PASS). FOLLOWING THE SECOND PASS, FOR THE TRUNNION COMMAND, THE
024047,001825:                                                                                                  #  OCDUT AND OCDUS ERROR COUNTER DRIVE BITS (CHAN 14 BITS 12, 11)
024048,001826:                                                                                                  #  ARE SET. THIS PROGRAM THEN EXITS TO THE CALLING PROGRAM.
024049,001827: 
024050,001828:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
024051,001829:                                                                                                  #  L TC RROUT (WITH RUPT INHIBITED) RROUT IS CALLED BY
024052,001830:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY, RRSONLY, AND DODES
024053,001831:

024056,001834:                                                                                                  #  (1ST PASS = 0), RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE SET (CHAN 12 BIT 2).
024057,001835:

024059,001837:                                                                                                  #  MAGSUB

024062,001840:                                                                                                  #  NONE

024139,001917:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRDESSM                                                  R (HALF-UNIT) IN RRTARGET. REMODES IF
024140,001918: 
024141,001919:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
024142,001920:                                                                                                  #  THIS INTERPRETIVE ROUTINE WILL DESIGNATE, IF DESIRED ANGLES ARE
024143,001921:                                                                                                  #  WITHIN THE LIMITS OF EITHER MODE, TO A LINE-OF SIGHT (LOS) VECTOR
024144,001922:                                                                                                  #  (HALF-UNIT) KNOWN WITH RESPECT TO THE STABLE MEMBER PRESENT
024145,001923:                                                                                                  #  ORIENTATION. INITIALLY THE IMU CDU:S ARE READ AND CONTROL
024146,001924:                                                                                                  #  TRANSFERRED TO SMNB TO TRANSFORM THE LOS VECTOR FROM STABLE
024147,001925:                                                                                                  #  MEMBER TO NAVIGATION BASE COORDINATES (SEE STG MEMO -699)
024148,001926:                                                                                                  #  RRANGLES IS THEN CALLED TO CALCULATE THE RR GIMBAL ANGLES,
024149,001927:                                                                                                  #  TRUNNION AND SHAFT, FOR BOTH THE PRESENT AND ALTERNATE MODE.
024150,001928:                                                                                                  #  RRLIMCHK IS CALLED TO SEE IF THE ANGLES CALCULATED FOR THE
024151,001929:                                                                                                  #  PRESENT MODE ARE WITHIN LIMITS. IF WITHIN LIMITS, THE RETURN
024152,001930:                                                                                                  #  LOCATION IS INCREMENTED, INASMUCH AS NO VEHICLE MANEUVER IS
024153,001931:                                                                                                  #  REQUIRED, BEFORE EXITING TO STARTDES. IF NOT WITHIN LIMITS OF THE
024154,001932:                                                                                                  #  CURRENT MODE, TRYSWS IS CALLED. FOLLOWING INVERTING OF THE RR
024155,001933:                                                                                                  #  ANTENNA MODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 12), RRLIMCHK IS CALLED
024156,001934:                                                                                                  #  TO SEE IF THE ANGLES CALCULATED FOR THE ALTERNATE MODE ARE WITHIN
024157,001935:                                                                                                  #  LIMITS. IF YES, THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG IS AGAIN INVERTED,
024158,001936:                                                                                                  #  THE REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14) SET, AND THE RETURN LOCATION
024159,001937:                                                                                                  #  INCREMENTED, TO INDICATE NO VEHICLE MANEUVER IS REQUIRED, BEFORE
024160,001938:                                                                                                  #  EXITING TO STARTDES. IF THESE ANGLES ARE NOT WITHIN LIMITS
024161,001939:                                                                                                  #  OF THE ALTERNATE MODE, THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG (RADMODES
024162,001940:                                                                                                  #  BIT 12) IS INVERTED BEFORE RETURNING DIRECTLY TO THE CALLING PROGRAM
024163,001941:                                                                                                  #  TO INDICATE THAT A VEHICLE MANEUVER IS REQUIRED.
024164,001942: 
024165,001943:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
024166,001944:                                                                                                  #  L  STCALL  RRTARGET  (LOS HALF-UNIT VECTOR IN SM COORDINATES)
024167,001945:                                                                                                  #  L+1  RRDESSM
024168,001946:                                                                                                  #  L+2  BASIC  (VEHICLE MANEUVER REQUIRED)
024169,001947:                                                                                                  #  L+3  BASIC  (NO VEHICLE MANEUVER REQUIRED)
024170,001948: 
024171,001949:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
024172,001950:                                                                                                  #  RRTARGET, RADMODES
024173,001951: 
024174,001952:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
024175,001953:                                                                                                  #  READCDUS, SMNB, RRANGLES, RRLIMCHK, TRYSWS (ACTUALLY
024176,001954:                                                                                                  #  PART OF), RMODINV
024177,001955: 
024178,001956:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
024179,001957:                                                                                                  #     NONE
024180,001958: 
024181,001959:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
024182,001960: 
024183,001961:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  L+2 (NEITHER SET OF ANGLES ARE WITHIN LIMITS OF RELATED MODE)
024184,001962:                                                                                                  #  STARTDES (DESIGNATE POSSIBLE AT PRESENT VEHICLE ATTITUDE-RETURNS
024185,001963:                                                                                                  #  TO L+3 FROM STARTDES)                                                   CAN BE DONE IN PRESENT VEH ATTITUDE.
024186,001964: 
024187,001965: 25,2373           43020        RRDESSM            STQ      CLEAR                                 
024188,001966: 25,2374           01113                                    DESRET

024190,001968: 25,2375           00271                                    RRNBSW

024192,001970: 25,2377           47443                                    CDUTRIG                               
024193,001971: 25,2400           45175                           VLOAD    CALL                                  #  LOAD VECTOR AND CALL TRANSFORMATION
024194,001972: 25,2401           01102                                    RRTARGET                              
024195,001973: 25,2402           47575                                    *SMNB*

024198,001976: 25,2404           26133                                    RRANGLES                              #  ALTERNATE MODE.
024199,001977: 25,2405           77776                           EXIT
