024225,002003:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  STARTDES                                                 STORED AS A HALF-UNIT VECTOR IN RRTARGET
024226,002004: 
024227,002005:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_                                                 CKON IS DESIRED. BIT14 OF RADMODES IS
024228,002006:                                                                                                  #  STARTDES IS ENTERED WHEN WE ARE READY TO BEGIN DESIGNATION.             OR REPOSITION OPERATION. IN THIS
024229,002007:                                                                                                  #  BIT 14 OF RADMODES IS ALREADY SET IF A REMODE IS REQUIRED.              THE REPOSITION WILL BE INTERRUPTED.
024230,002008:                                                                                                  #  AT THIS TIME, THE RR ANTENNA MAY BE IN A REPOSITION                     GINS.
024231,002009:                                                                                                  #  OPERATION. IN THIS CASE, IF A REMODE IS REQUIRED IT MAY HAVE
024232,002010:                                                                                                  #  ALREADY BEGUN BUT IN ANY CASE THE REPOSITION WILL BE INTERRUPTED.
024233,002011:                                                                                                  #  OTHERWISE, THE REPOSITION WILL BE COMPLETED BEFORE 2-AXIS
024234,002012:                                                                                                  #  DESIGNATION BEGINS. INITIALLY DESCOUNT IS SET = 60 TO INDICATE
024235,002013:                                                                                                  #  THAT 30 SECONDS WILL BE ALLOWED FOR THE RR DATA GOOD INBIT
024236,002014:                                                                                                  #  (CHAN 33 BIT 4) IF LOCK-ON IS DESIRED (STATE BIT 5). BIT 10
024237,002015:                                                                                                  #  OF RADMODES IS SET TO SHOW THAT A DESIGNATE IS REQUIRED.
024238,002016:                                                                                                  #  THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS CHECKED. IF SET,
024239,002017:                                                                                                  #  THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L+3 OF THE CALLING PROGRAM (SEE RRDESSM
024240,002018:                                                                                                  #  AND RRDESNB). THE PROGRAM WILL BEGIN DESIGNATING TO THE DESIRED
024241,002019:                                                                                                  #  ANGLES FOLLOWING THE REPOSITION OR REMODE IF ONE WAS
024242,002020:                                                                                                  #  REQUESTED. IF THE REPOSITION FLAG IS NOT SET, SETRRECR IS CALLED
024243,002021:                                                                                                  #  WHICH SETS THE RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2)
024244,002022:                                                                                                  #  AND SETS LASTYCMD AND LASTXCMD = 0 TO INDICATE THE
024245,002023:                                                                                                  #  DIFFERENCE BETWEEN THE PRESENT AND DESIRED STATE OF THE ERROR
024246,002024:                                                                                                  #  COUNTERS. A 20 MILLISECOND WAITLIST CALL IS SET FOR BEGDES
024247,002025:                                                                                                  #  AFTER WHICH THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L+3 OF THE CALLING PROGRAM.
024248,002026: 
024249,002027:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
024250,002028:                                                                                                  #  FROM RRDESSM AND RRDESNB WHEN ANGLES WITHIN LIMITS.
024251,002029: 
024252,002030:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
024253,002031:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES, (SEE DODES)
024254,002032: 
024255,002033:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
024256,002034:                                                                                                  #  SETRRECR, WAITLIST
024257,002035: 
024258,002036:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
024259,002037:                                                                                                  #  BEGDES
024260,002038: 
024261,002039:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
024262,002040: 
024263,002041:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  L+3 OF CALLING PROGRAM (SEE RRDESSM)
024264,002042:                                                                                                  #  L+2 OF CALLING PROGRAM (SEE RRDESNB)
024265,002043:

024396,002174:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  BEGDES
024397,002175: 
024398,002176:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
024399,002177:                                                                                                  #  BEGDES CHECKS VARIOUS DESIGNATE REQUESTS AND REQUESTS THE
024400,002178:                                                                                                  #  ACTUAL RR DESIGNATION. INITIALLY A CHECK IS MADE TO SEE IF A
024401,002179:                                                                                                  #  REMODE (RADMODES BIT 14) IS REQUESTED OR IN PROGRESS. IF SO,
024402,002180:                                                                                                  #  CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO STDESIG AFTER ROUTINE REMODE IS
024403,002181:                                                                                                  #  EXECUTED. IF NO REMODE, STDESIG IS IMMEDIATELY CALLED WHERE
024404,002182:                                                                                                  #  FIRST THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS CHECKED. IF
024405,002183:                                                                                                  #  PRESENT, THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 10) IS REMOVED
024406,002184:                                                                                                  #  AFTER WHICH THE PROGRAM EXITS TO RDBADEND. IF THE REPOSITION
024407,002185:                                                                                                  #  FLAG IS NOT PRESENT, THE CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
024408,002186:                                                                                                  #  BIT 15) IS CHECKED. IF PRESENT, ON EXECUTIVE CALL IS IMMEDIATELY
024409,002187:                                                                                                  #  MADE FOR DODES AFTER WHICH A .5 SECOND WAIT IS INITIATED BEFORE
024410,002188:                                                                                                  #  REPEATING AT STDESIG. IF THE RR SEARCH ROUTINE (LRS24.1) IS DESIGNATING
024411,002189:                                                                                                  #  TO A NEW POINT (NEWPTFLG SET) THE CURRENT DESIGNATE TASK IS TERMINATED.
024412,002190:                                                                                                  #  IF CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE IS NOT WANTED, THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
024413,002191:                                                                                                  #  BIT 10) IS CHECKED. IF NOT PRESENT, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO ENDRADAR TO
024414,002192:                                                                                                  #  CHECK RR CDU FAIL BEFORE RETURNING TO THE CALLING PROGRAM. IF DESIGNATE
024415,002193:                                                                                                  #  IS STILL REQUIRED, DESCOUNT IS CHECKED TO SEE IF THE 30 SECONDS HAS
024416,002194:                                                                                                  #  EXPIRED BEFORE RECEIVING THE RR DATA GOOD (CHAN 33 BIT 4)
024417,002195:                                                                                                  #  SIGNAL. IF OUT OF TIME, PROGRAM ALARM 00503 IS REQUESTED, THE
024418,002196:                                                                                                  #  RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE AND RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE
024419,002197:                                                                                                  #  (CHAN 12 BITS 14,2) BITS REMOVED, AND THE DESIGNATE FLAG
024420,002198:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 10) REMOVED BEFORE EXITING TO RDBADEND. IF
024421,002199:                                                                                                  #  TIME HAS NOT EXPIRED, DESCOUNT IS DECREMENTED, THE
024422,002200:                                                                                                  #  EXECUTIVE CALL MADE FOR DODES, AND A .5 SECOND WAIT INITIATED
024423,002201:                                                                                                  #  BEFORE REPEATING THIS PROCEDURE AT STDESIG.
024424,002202: 
024425,002203:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
024426,002204:                                                                                                  #  WAITLIST CALL FROM STARTDES
024427,002205:                                                                                                  #  TCF BEGDES FROM DORREPOS
024428,002206:                                                                                                  #  TC STDESIG RETURNING, FROM REMODE
024429,002207: 
024430,002208:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
024431,002209:                                                                                                  #  DESCOUNT, RADMODES
024432,002210: 
024433,002211:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
024434,002212:                                                                                                  #  ENDRADAR, FINDVAC
024435,002213: 
024436,002214:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_  DODES
024437,002215: 
024438,002216:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  PROGRAM ALARM 00503 (30 SECONDS HAVE EXPIRED) WITH NO RR DATA
024439,002217:                                                                                                  #  GOOD (CHAN 33 BIT 4) RECEIVED WHEN LOCK-ON (STATE BIT 5) WAS REQUESTED.
024440,002218: 
024441,002219:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  TASKOVER (SEARCH PATTERN DESIGNATING TO NEW POINT)
024442,002220:                                                                                                  #  ENDRADAR (NO DESIGNATE - RADMODES BIT 10)
024443,002221:                                                                                                  #  RDBADEND (REPOSITION OR 30 SECONDS EXPIRED)
024444,002222: 
024445,002223: 25,2573           40110        BEGDES             CS       RADMODES

024492,002270:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  DODES
024493,002271: 
024494,002272:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
024495,002273:                                                                                                  #  DODES CALCULATES AND REQUESTS ISSUANCE OF RR GYRO TORQUE
024496,002274:                                                                                                  #  COMMANDS. INITIALLY THE CURRENT RR CDU ANGLES ARE STORED AND
024497,002275:                                                                                                  #  THE LOS HALF-UNIT VECTOR TRANSFORMED FROM STABLE MEMBER TO
024498,002276:                                                                                                  #  NAVIGATION BASE COORDINATES VIA SMNB IF NECESSARY. THE
024499,002277:                                                                                                  #  SHAFT AND TRUNNION COMMANDS ARE THEN CALCULATED AS FOLLOWS_
024500,002278:                                                                                                  #  + SHAFT = LOS  . (COS(S), 0, -SIN (S)) (DOT PRODUCT)
024501,002279:                                                                                                  #  -TRUNNION = LOS  . (SIN (T) SIN (S), COS (T), SIN (T) COS (S) )
024502,002280:                                                                                                  #  THE SIGN OF THE SHAFT COMMAND IS THEN REVERSED IF IN MODE 2
024503,002281:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 12) BECAUSE A RELAY IN THE RR REVERSES THE
024504,002282:                                                                                                  #  POLARITY OF THE COMMAND. AT RRSCALUP EACH COMMAND IS
024505,002283:                                                                                                  #  SCALED AND IF EITHER, OR BOTH, OF THE COMMANDS IS GREATER THAN
024506,002284:                                                                                                  #  .5 DEGREES, MPAC +1 IS SET POSITIVE. IF A CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE
024507,002285:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 15) IS DESIRED AND THE SEARCH ROUTINE IS NOT OPERATING,
024508,002286:                                                                                                  #  THE RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 14) IS CLEARED AND RROUT
024509,002287:                                                                                                  #  CALLED TO PUT OUT THE COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION (RADMODES BIT 11)
024510,002288:                                                                                                  #  IS IN PROGRESS. IF A CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE AND THE SEARCH ROUTINE IS
024511,002289:                                                                                                  #  OPERATING (SRCHOPT FLAG SET) THE TRACK ENABLE IS NOT CLEARED. IF NO
024512,002290:                                                                                                  #  CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE AND BOTH COMMANDS ARE NOT LESS THAN .5 DEGREES AS
024513,002291:                                                                                                  #  INDICATED BY MPAC +1, THE RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 14) IS
024514,002292:                                                                                                  #  CLEARED AND RROUT CALLED TO PUT OUT THE COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION
024515,002293:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 11) IS IN PROGRESS. IF BOTH COMMANDS ARE LESS THAN .5
024516,002294:                                                                                                  #  DEGREES AS INDICATED BY MPAC+1, THE RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE BIT
024517,002295:                                                                                                  #  (CHAN 12 BIT 14) IS CLEARED AND RROUT CALLED TO PUT OUT THE
024518,002296:                                                                                                  #  COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION (RADMODES BIT 11) IS IN
024519,002297:                                                                                                  #  PROGRESS. IF BOTH COMMANDS ARE LESS THAN .5 DEGREES, THE
024520,002298:                                                                                                  #  LOCK-ON FLAG (STATE BIT 5) IS CHECKED. IF NOT PRESENT, THE
024521,002299:                                                                                                  #  DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 10) IS CLEARED, THE RR ERROR
024522,002300:                                                                                                  #  COUNTER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2) IS CLEARED, AND ENDOFJOB
024523,002301:                                                                                                  #  CALLED. IF LOCK-ON IS DESIRED, THE RR AUTO TRACKER (CHAN 12
024524,002302:                                                                                                  #  BIT 14) IS ENABLED FOLLOWED BY A CHECK OF THE RECEIPT OF THE
024525,002303:                                                                                                  #  RR DATA GOOD (CHAN 33 BIT 4) SIGNAL. IF RR DATA GOOD
024526,002304:                                                                                                  #  PRESENT, THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 10) IS CLEARED,
024527,002305:                                                                                                  #  THE RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2) IS CLEARED,
024528,002306:                                                                                                  #  AND ENDOFJOB CALLED. IF RR DATA GOOD IS NOT PRESENT, RROUT
024529,002307:                                                                                                  #  IS CALLED TO PUT OUT THE COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION
024530,002308:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 11) IS IN PROGRESS AFTER WHICH THE JOB IS TERMINATED
024531,002309:                                                                                                  #  VIA ENDOFJOB.
024532,002310: 
024533,002311:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
024534,002312:                                                                                                  #  EXECUTIVE CALL EVERY .5 SECONDS FROM BEGDES.
024535,002313: 
024536,002314:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
024537,002315:                                                                                                  #  RRTARGET (HALF-UNIT LOS VECTOR IN EITHER SM OR NB COORDINATES),
024538,002316:                                                                                                  #  LOKONSW (STATE BIT 5), RRNBSW (STATE BIT 6), RADMODES
024539,002317: 
024540,002318:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
024541,002319:                                                                                                  #  READCDUS, SMNB, CDULOGIC, MAGSUB, RROUT
024542,002320:

Page 559

024545,002323:                                                                                                  #  NONE

025323,003101:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME: LRS22.1 (DATA READ SUBROUTINE 1)
025324,003102:                                                                                                  #  MOD. NO.: 1       BY:  P. VOLANTE  SDC           DATE:  11-15-66
025325,003103: 
025326,003104: 
025327,003105:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
025328,003106: 
025329,003107:                                                                                                  #  1) READS RENDEZVOUS RADAR RANGE AND RANGE-RATE,TRUNION AND SHAFT ANGLES,THREE CDU VALUES AND TIME. CONVERTS THIS
025330,003108:                                                                                                  #  DATA AND LEAVES IT FOR THE MEASUREMENT INCORPORATION ROUTINE (LSR22.3). CHECKS FOR THE RR DATA GOOD DISCRETE,FOR
025331,003109:                                                                                                  #  RR REPOSITION AND RR CDU FAIL
025332,003110: 
025333,003111:                                                                                                  #  2) COMPARES RADAR LOS WITH LOS COMPUTED FROM STATE VECTORS TO SEE IF THEY ARE WITHIN THREE DEGREES
025334,003112: 
025335,003113: 
025336,003114:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE: BANKCALL FOR LRS22.1
025337,003115: 
025338,003116: 
025339,003117:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED:
025340,003118: 
025341,003119:                                                                                                  #         RRRDOT   LPS20.1
025342,003120:                                                                                                  #         RRRANGE  BANKCALL
025343,003121:                                                                                                  #         RADSTALL CDULOGIC
025344,003122:                                                                                                  #         RRNB     SMNB
025345,003123:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT: RETURN TO CALLER+1 WITH MPAC SET TO +0
025346,003124: 
025347,003125: 
025348,003126:                                                                                                  #  ERROR EXITS: RETURN TO CALLER+1 WITH ERROR CODE STORED IN MPAC AS FOLLOWS:
025349,003127: 
025350,003128:                                                                                                  #               00001-ERROR EXIT 1-RR DATA NO GOOD (NO RR DATA GOOD DISCRETE OR RR CDU FAIL OR RR REPOSITION)
025351,003129:                                                                                                  #               00002-ERROR EXIT 2-RR LOS NOT WITHIN THREE DEGREES OF LOS COMPUTED FROM STATE VECTORS
025352,003130: 
025353,003131: 
025354,003132:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS:  521-COULD NOT READ RADAR DATA (RR DATA GOOD DISCRETE NOT PRESENT BEFORE AND AFTER READING THE RADAR)
025355,003133:                                                                                                  #   (THIS ALARM IS ISSUED BY THE RADAREAD SUBROUTINE WHICH IS ENTERED FROM A RADARUPT)
025356,003134: 
025357,003135: 
025358,003136:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT: RRLOSVEC- THE RR LINE-OF-SIGHT VECTOR(USED BY LRS22.2)-A HALF-UNIT VECTOR
025359,003137:                                                                                                  #          RM- THE RR RANGE READING(TO THE CSM) DP, IN METERS SCALED B-29(USED BY LRS22.2 AND LRS22.3)
025360,003138: 
025361,003139:                                                                                                  #     ALL OF THE FOLLOWING OUTPUTS ARE USED BY LRS22.3:
025362,003140: 
025363,003141:                                                                                                  #          RDOTM- THE RR RANGE-RATE READING,DP, IN METERS PER CENTISECOND, SCALED B-7
025364,003142:                                                                                                  #          RRTRUN-RR TRUNION ANGLE,DP,IN REVOLUTIONS,SCALED B0
025365,003143:                                                                                                  #          RRSHAFT-RR SHAFT ANGLE,DP,IN REVOLUTIONS,SCALED B0
025366,003144:                                                                                                  #          AIG,AMG,AOG-THE CDU ANGLES,THREE SP WORDS
025367,003145:                                                                                                  #          MKTIME-THE TIME OF THE RR READING,DP,IN CENTISECONDS
025368,003146: 
025369,003147: 
025370,003148:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
025371,003149: 
025372,003150:                                                                                                  #     RNRAD,THE RADAR READ COUNTER FROM WHICH IS OBTAINED:
025373,003151:

Page 580 

025375,003153:                                                                                                  #      1)RR RANGE SCALED 9.38 FT. PER BIT ON THE LOW SCALE AND 75.04 FT. PER BIT ON THE HIGH SCALE
025376,003154:                                                                                                  #      2)RR RANGE RATE,SCALED .6278 FT./SEC. PER BIT
025377,003155: 
025378,003156:                                                                                                  #     THE CDU ANGLES FROM CDUX,CDUY,CDUZ AND TIME1 AND TIME2
025379,003157: 
025380,003158: 
025381,003159:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS:  LRS22.1X,A,L,Q,PUSHLIST

025561,003339:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME - LSR22.3                                                  DATE - 29 MAY 1967
025562,003340:                                                                                                  #  MOD. NO 3                                                               LOG SECTION - P20-25
025563,003341:                                                                                                  #  MOD. BY - DANFORTH                                                      ASSEMBLY LEMP20S REV 10
025564,003342: 
025565,003343:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
025566,003344: 
025567,003345:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE COMPUTES THE B-VECTORS AND DELTA Q FOR EACH OF THE QUANTITIES MEASURED BY THE RENDEZVOUS
025568,003346:                                                                                                  #  RADAR.(RANGE,RANGE RATE,SHAFT AND TRUNNION ANGLES). THE ROUTINE CALLS THE INCORP1 AND INCORP2 ROUTINES
025569,003347:                                                                                                  #  WHICH COMPUTE THE DEVIATIONS AND CORRECT THE STATE VECTOR.
025570,003348: 
025571,003349:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE
025572,003350:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE IS PART OF P20 RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION FOR THE LM COMPUTER O NLY. THE ROUTINE IS ENTERED FROM
025573,003351:                                                                                                  #  R22LEM  ONLY AND RETURNS DIRECTLY TO R22LEM  FOLLOWING SUCCESSFUL INCORPORATION OF MEASURED DATA. IF THE
025574,003352:                                                                                                  #  COMPUTED STATE VECTOR DEVIATIONS EXCEED THE MAXIMUM PERMITTED. THE ROUTINE RETURNS TO R22LEM  TO DISPLAY
025575,003353:                                                                                                  #  THE DEVIATIONS. IF THE ASTRONAUT ACCEPTS THE DATA R22LEM  RETURNS TO    LSR22.3 TO INCORPORATE THE
025576,003354:                                                                                                  #  DEVIATIONS INTO THE STATE VECTOR. IF THE ASTRONAUT REJECTS THE DEVIATIONS, NO MORE MEASUREMENTS ARE
025577,003355:                                                                                                  #  PROCESSED FOR THIS MARK,I.E.,R22LEM  GETS THE NEXT MARK.
025578,003356: 
025579,003357: 
025580,003358:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
025581,003359:                                                                                                  #   WLINIT     LGCUPDTE     INTEGRV     INCORP1     ARCTAN
025582,003360:                                                                                                  #   GETULC     RARARANG     INCORP2     NBSM        INTSTALL
025583,003361: 
025584,003362:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
025585,003363:                                                                                                  #   CORRECTED LM OR CSM STATE VECTOR (PERMANENT)
025586,003364:                                                                                                  #   NUMBER OF MARKS INCORPORATED IN MARKCTR
025587,003365:                                                                                                  #   MAGNITUDE OF POSITION DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP METERS B-29
025588,003366:                                                                                                  #   MAGNITUDE OF VELOCITY DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP +2 M/CSEC B-7
025589,003367:                                                                                                  #   UPDATED W-MATRIX
025590,003368: 
025591,003369: 
025592,003370:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
025593,003371:                                                                                                  #   LM AND CSM STATE VECTORS
025594,003372:                                                                                                  #   W-MATRIX
025595,003373:                                                                                                  #   MARK TIME IN MKTIME
025596,003374:                                                                                                  #   RADAR RANGE IN RM METERS B-29
025597,003375:                                                                                                  #         RANGE RATE IN RDOTM METERS/CSES B-7
025598,003376:                                                                                                  #         SHAFT ANGLE IN RRSHAFT REVS.B0
025599,003377:                                                                                                  #         TRUNNION ANGLE IN RRTRUN REVS. B0
025600,003378:                                                                                                  #   GIMBAL ANGLES  INNER IN AIG
025601,003379:                                                                                                  #                  MIDDLE IN AMG
025602,003380:                                                                                                  #                  OUTER IN AOG
025603,003381:                                                                                                  #   REFSMMAT
025604,003382:                                                                                                  #   RENDWFLG
025605,003383:                                                                                                  #   NOANGFLG
025606,003384:                                                                                                  #   VEHUPFLG

025608,003386:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS

026001,003779: 26,3142           50614                                    R22LEM93                              
026002,003780:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
026003,003781: 
026004,003782:                                                                                                  #  LSR22.4 IS THE ENTRY TO PERFORM LUNAR SURFACE NAVIGATION FOR THE LM
026005,003783:                                                                                                  #  COMPUTER ONLY. THIS ROUTINE COMPUTES THE B-VECTORS AND DELTA Q FOR RANGE
026006,003784:                                                                                                  #  AND RANGE RATE MEASURED BY THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR
026007,003785: 
026008,003786:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
026009,003787:                                                                                                  #   INSTALL   LGCUPDTE  INCORP1   RP-TO-R
026010,003788:                                                                                                  #   INTEGRV   GETULC    INCORP2
026011,003789: 
026012,003790:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
026013,003791:                                                                                                  #   CORRECTED CSM STATE VECTOR (PERMANENT)
026014,003792:                                                                                                  #   NUMBER OF MARKS INCORPORATED IN MARKCTR
026015,003793:                                                                                                  #   MAGNITUDE OF POSITION DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP METERS B-29
026016,003794:                                                                                                  #   MAGNITUDE OF VELOCITY DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP +2 M/CSEC B-7
026017,003795:                                                                                                  #   UPDATED W-MATRIX
026018,003796: 
026019,003797:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
026020,003798:                                                                                                  #   LM AND CSM STATE VECTORS
026021,003799:                                                                                                  #   W-MATRIX
026022,003800:                                                                                                  #   MARK TIME IN MKTIME
026023,003801:                                                                                                  #   RADAR RANGE IN RM METERS B-29
026024,003802:                                                                                                  #         RANGE RATE IN RDOTM METERS/CSEC B-7
026025,003803:                                                                                                  #   VEHUPFLG
026026,003804:

Page 594 

026028,003806: 26,3143           77624        LSR22.4            CALL                                           
026029,003807: 26,3144           27412                                    INTSTALL

026227,004005:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME LRS24.1   RR SEARCH ROUTINE
026228,004006:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO  0        BY  P VOLANTE  SDC          DATE 1-15-67
026229,004007: 
026230,004008: 
026231,004009:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
026232,004010: 
026233,004011:                                                                                                  #  DRIVES THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR IN A HEXAGONAL SEARCH PATTERN ABOUT THE LOS TO THE CSM (COMPUTED FROM THE CSM AND LM
026234,004012:                                                                                                  #  STATE VECTORS) CHECKING FOR THE DATA GOOD DISCRETE AND MONITORING THE ANGLE BETWEEN THE RADAR BORESIGHT AND THE
026235,004013:                                                                                                  #  LM +Z AXIS. IF THIS ANGLE EXCEEDS 30 DEGREES THE PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE ROUTINE IS CALLED TO PERFORM AN
026236,004014:                                                                                                  #  ATTITUDE MANEUVER.
026237,004015: 
026238,004016: 
026239,004017:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE - BANKCALL FOR LRS24.1
026240,004018: 
026241,004019: 
026242,004020:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
026243,004021: 
026244,004022:                                                                                                  #        LEMCONIC      R61LEM
026245,004023:                                                                                                  #        CSMCONIC      RRDESSM
026246,004024:                                                                                                  #        JOBDELAY      FLAGDOWN
026247,004025:                                                                                                  #        WAITLIST      FLAGUP
026248,004026:                                                                                                  #        RRNB          BANKCALL
026249,004027: 
026250,004028: 
026251,004029:                                                                                                  #  EXIT -  TO ENDOFJOB WHEN THE SEARCH FLAG (SRCHOPT) IS NOT SET
026252,004030: 
026253,004031: 
026254,004032:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
026255,004033: 
026256,004034:                                                                                                  #      DATAGOOD (SP)-FOR DISPLAY IN R1- 00000 INDICATES NO LOCKON
026257,004035:                                                                                                  #                                       11111 INDICATES LOCKON ACHIEVED
026258,004036:                                                                                                  #      OMEGAD   (SP)-FOR DISPLAY IN R2- ANGLE BETWEEN RR BORESIGHT VECTOR AND THE SPACECRAFT +Z AXIS
026259,004037: 
026260,004038:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
026261,004039:                                                                                                  #     SEARCH FLAG MUST BE SET
026262,004040:                                                                                                  #     LM AND CSM STATE VECTORS AND REFSMMAT MATRIX
026263,004041:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
026264,004042: 
026265,004043:                                                                                                  #     RLMSRCH      UXVECT
026266,004044:                                                                                                  #     VXRLM        UYVECT
026267,004045:                                                                                                  #     LOSDESRD     NSRCHPNT
026268,004046:                                                                                                  #     DATAGOOD     OMEGAD
026269,004047:                                                                                                  #     MPAC         PUSHLIST
026270,004048: 
026271,004049: 26,3405                                           COUNT*   $$/LRS24                              
026272,004050: 26,3405           34755        LRS24.1            CAF      ZERO                                  
026273,004051: 26,3406           55734                           TS       NSRCHPNT                              #  SET SEARCH PATTERN POINT COUNTER TO ZERO
026274,004052: 26,3407           34736        CHKSRCH            CAF      BIT14                                 #  ISSUE AUTO TRACK ENABLE TO RADAR
026275,004053: 26,3410           00006                           EXTEND                                         
026276,004054:

Page 599 

026278,004056: 26,3411           05012                           WOR      CHAN12

026281,004059: 26,3414           00006                           EXTEND

026545,004323:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME: R29  (RENDEZVOUS RADAR DESIGNATE DURING POWERED FLIGHT)
026546,004324:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO. 2       BY H. BLAIR-SMITH       JULY 2, 1968.
026547,004325: 
026548,004326: 
026549,004327:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION:
026550,004328: 
026551,004329:                                                                                                  #  DESIGNATES THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR TOWARD THE COMPUTED LOS TO THE CSM, WITH THE CHIEF OBJECTIVE OF OBTAINING RANGE
026552,004330:                                                                                                  #  AND RANGE RATE DATA AT 2-SECOND INTERVALS FOR TRANSMISSION TO THE GROUND.  WHEN THE RR IS WITHIN .5 DEGREE OF
026553,004331:                                                                                                  #  THE COMPUTED LOS, TRACKING IS ENABLED, AND DESIGNATION CONTINUES UNTIL THE DATA-GOOD DISCRETE IS RECEIVED.  AT
026554,004332:                                                                                                  #  THAT POINT, DESIGNATION CEASES AND A RADAR-READING ROUTINE TAKES OVER, PREPARING A CONSISTENT SET OF DATA FOR
026555,004333:                                                                                                  #  DOWN TELEMETRY.  THE SET INCLUDES RANGE, RANGE RATE, MARK TIME, TWO RR CDU ANGLES, THREE IMUCDU ANGLES, AND AN
026556,004334:                                                                                                  #  INDICATOR WHICH IS 1 WHEN THE SET IS CONSISTENT AND 0 OTHERWISE.  THE INDICATOR IS IN TRKMKCNT.
026557,004335: 
026558,004336:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:  BEGUN EVERY 2 SECONDS AS AN INTEGRAL PART OF SERVICER
026559,004337: 
026560,004338: 
026561,004339:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED:
026562,004340: 
026563,004341:                                                                                                  #  REMODE   RRTONLY
026564,004342:                                                                                                  #  UNIT     MPACVBUF
026565,004343:                                                                                                  #  QUICTRIG AX*SR*T
026566,004344:                                                                                                  #  SPSIN    SPCOS
026567,004345:                                                                                                  #  SETRRECR RROUT
026568,004346:                                                                                                  #  RRRDOT   RRRANGE
026569,004347: 
026570,004348: 
026571,004349:                                                                                                  #  EXIT:  TO NOR29NOW, IN SERVICER.
026572,004350: 
026573,004351: 
026574,004352:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT:  (ALL FOR DOWNLINK)
026575,004353: 
026576,004354:                                                                                                  #  RM       RDOTM                  (RAW)
026577,004355:                                                                                                  #  AIG      AMG
026578,004356:                                                                                                  #  AOG      TRKMKCNT               TRKMKCNT = 00001 IF SET IS CONSISTENT,
026579,004357:                                                                                                  #  TANGNB   TANGNB +1              OTHERWISE TRKMKCNT = 00000.
026580,004358:                                                                                                  #  MKTIME
026581,004359:

Page 606 

026583,004361: 
026584,004362:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
026585,004363: 
026586,004364:                                                                                                  #  NOR29FLG READRFLG               (TO 1 AND 0 BY FRESH START)  (RESET NOR29FLG TO LET SERVICER RUN R29)
026587,004365:                                                                                                  #  PIPTIME  RADMODES (BIT 10)      (BIT SET TO 0 BY FRESH START)
026588,004366:                                                                                                  #  R(CSM)   V(CSM)
026589,004367:                                                                                                  #  R        V                      (PIPTIME THRU V BY AVE G IN SERVICER)
026590,004368: 
026591,004369: 
026592,004370:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS:
026593,004371: 
026594,004372:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES (BIT 10)
026595,004373:                                                                                                  #  LOSSM    LOSVDT/4       (= RRTARGET & LOSVEL)
026596,004374:                                                                                                  #  SAVECDUT OLDESFLG       (SAVECDUT = MLOSV)
026597,004375:                                                                                                  #  LOSCMFLG READRFLG
026598,004376: 
026599,004377: 
026600,004378:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS:  NONE.
026601,004379: 
026602,004380: 
026603,004381:                                                                                                  #  COMPONENT JOBS AND TASKS:
026604,004382: 
026605,004383:                                                                                                  #  INITIALIZING, IF RR IS FOUND TO BE IN MODE 1:  JOB R29REMOJ AND TASK REMODE;  ALWAYS: TASK PREPOS29.
026606,004384:                                                                                                  #  DESIGNATING:  TASK BEGDES29 & JOB R29DODES.
026607,004385:                                                                                                  #  RADAR READING:  TASK R29READ AND JOB R29RDJOB.  ALL JOBS ARE NOVAC TYPE.
026608,004386: 
026609,004387: 
026610,004388: 33,2045                                           BANK     33                                    
026611,004389: 33,2000                                           SETLOC   R29/SERV                              
026612,004390: 33,2000                                           BANK                                           
026613,004391: 
026614,004392: 33,2045                                           COUNT*   $$/R29                                
026615,004393: 
026616,004394: 33,2045     5014               NR29&RDR           EQUALS   EBANK5                                
026617,004395:

Page 607 

026619,004397:                                                                                                  #  SERVICER COMES TO R29 FROM "R29?" IF NOR29FLG, READRFLG, RRREMODE, RRCDUZRO, RRREPOS, AND DISPLAY-INERTIAL-DATA
026620,004398:                                                                                                  #  ARE ALL RESET, AND THE RR IS IN LGC MODE (OFTEN CONFUSINGLY CALLED AUTO MODE).
026621,004399: 
026622,004400: 33,2045           40110        R29                CS       RADMODES                              
026623,004401: 33,2046           74742                           MASK     BIT10                                 
026624,004402: 33,2047           00006                           EXTEND                                         
026625,004403: 33,2050           12123                           BZF      R29.LOS                               #  BRANCH IF DESIGNATION IS ALREADY ON.
026626,004404: 
026627,004405: 33,2051           00004                           INHINT                                         
026628,004406: 33,2052           26110                           ADS      RADMODES                              #  SHOW THAT DESIGNATION IS NOW ON.
026629,004407: 33,2053           44736                           CS       BIT14                                 
026630,004408: 33,2054           00006                           EXTEND

026632,004410: 33,2056           44740                           CS       LOSCMBIT                              
026633,004411: 33,2057           70076                           MASK     FLAGWRD2                              
026634,004412: 33,2060           54076                           TS       FLAGWRD2                              #  CLEAR LOSCMFLG TO SHOW DES. LOOP IS OFF.
026635,004413: 33,2061           44753                           CS       OLDESBIT                              
026636,004414: 33,2062           70074                           MASK     STATE                                 
026637,004415: 33,2063           54074                           TS       STATE                                 #  SHOW THAT DES. LOOP IS NOT REQUESTED.
026638,004416: 33,2064           04616                           TC       BANKCALL                              
026639,004417: 33,2065           52156                           CADR     SETRRECR                              #  ENABLE RR ERROR COUNTERS.
026640,004418: 33,2066           34740                           CA       BIT12                                 
026641,004419: 33,2067           70110                           MASK     RADMODES                              
026642,004420: 33,2070           10000                           CCS      A                                     #  TEST RR MODE BIT.
026643,004421: 33,2071           12104                           TCF      SETPRPOS                              #  MODE 2.
026644,004422: 
026645,004423: 33,2072           35031                           CA       PRIO21                                #  MODE 1; MUST REMODE.
026646,004424: 33,2073           05072                           TC       NOVAC                                 
026647,004425: 33,2074  E7,1454                                  EBANK=   LOSCOUNT                              
026648,004426: 33,2074           02113 66067                     2CADR    R29REM0J                              #  NEEDS OWN JOB TO RADSTALL IN.
026649,004427: 
026650,004428: 33,2076           44742                           CS       BIT10                                 
026651,004429: 33,2077           70110                           MASK     RADMODES                              #  CLEAR DESIGNATE FLAG IN RADMODES
026652,004430: 33,2100           54110                           TS       RADMODES                              #  BEFORE CALLING REMODE
026653,004431: 33,2101           34736                           CA       BIT14                                 
026654,004432: 33,2102           26110                           ADS      RADMODES                              #   SHOW THAT REMODING IS ON.
026655,004433: 33,2103           12623                           TCF      NOR29NOW                              #  CONTINUE SERVICER FUNCTIONS.
026656,004434: 
026657,004435: 33,2104           34753        SETPRPOS           CA       ONE                                   
026658,004436: 33,2105           05203                           TC       WAITLIST                              
026659,004437: 33,2106  E7,1454                                  EBANK=   LOSCOUNT                              
026660,004438: 33,2106           03601 52067                     2CADR    PREPOS29                              #  TASK TO SET TRUNNION ANGLE TO -180 DEG.
026661,004439: 
026662,004440: 33,2110           34741                           CA       BIT11                                 
026663,004441: 33,2111           26110                           ADS      RADMODES                              #  SHOW THAT REPOSITIONING IS ON.
026664,004442: 33,2112           12623                           TCF      NOR29NOW                              
026665,004443:

Page 608 

026667,004445:                                                                                                  #  FORCE RENDEZVOUS RADAR INTO MODE 2.
026668,004446: 
026669,004447: 33,2113           34753        R29REM0J           CA       ONE                                   
026670,004448: 33,2114           05203                           TC       WAITLIST                              
026671,004449: 33,2115  E7,1454                                  EBANK=   LOSCOUNT                              
026672,004450: 33,2115           02171 52067                     2CADR    REMODE                                #  REMODE MUST RUN AS A TASK.
026673,004451: 33,2117           04616                           TC       BANKCALL                              #  WAIT FOR END OF REMODING.
026674,004452: 33,2120           17667                           CADR     RADSTALL                              
026675,004453: 
026676,004454: 33,2121           15155                           TCF      ENDOFJOB                              #  BAD EXIT CAN'T HAPPEN.
026677,004455: 33,2122           15155                           TCF      ENDOFJOB                              
026678,004456: 
026679,004457:                                                                                                  #  TASK TO PREPOSITION THE RR TRUNNION ANGLE TO -180 DEG.
026680,004458: 
026681,004459: 25,2000                                           SETLOC   R29S1                                 
026682,004460: 25,2000                                           BANK                                           
026683,004461:

026689,004467: 25,3606           15261                           TCF      TASKOVER                              
026690,004468:

026712,004490:                                                                                                  #  LOSCMFLG=0 MEANS THAT THE DESIGNATION IS READY FOR NEW DATA.  SETTING LOSCMFLG MAKES IT GO AWAY SO SETUP29D CAN
026713,004491:                                                                                                  #  START IT UP WHEN THE DATA IS IN PLACE.

026787,004565:                                                                                                  #  R29DODES:  RR DESIGNATION LOOP FOR R29
026788,004566: 
026789,004567:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE DOES MUCH THE SAME THING AS DODES, BUT A GREAT DEAL FASTER.  IT TAKES THE NON-UNITIZED LOS VECTOR
026790,004568:                                                                                                  #  IN STABLE MEMBER COORDINATES (LOSSM) AND A DELTA-LOS IN SM AXES (LOSVDT/4) WHICH IS 1/2 SEC TIMES LOS VELOCITY,
026791,004569:                                                                                                  #  AND DEVELOPS THE SHAFT AND TRUNNION COMMANDS USING SINGLE PRECISION AS MUCH AS POSSIBLE, AND INTERPRETIVE NOT AT
026792,004570:                                                                                                  #  ALL.  THE UNIT(LOSSM + LOSVEL * 1 SEC) IS COMPUTED IN DP AND TRANSFORMED TO NAV BASE COORDINATES IN DOUBLE PRE-
026793,004571:                                                                                                  #  CISION (USING SP SINES AND COSINES OF CDU ANGLES), AND THE REST IS DONE IN SP.
026794,004572: 
026795,004573:                                                                                                  #  THE FUNCTIONAL DIFFERENCE IS THAT R29DODES ALWAYS CLEARS LOSCMFLG WHEN IT ENDS, AND IT STARTS UP THE R29READ
026796,004574:                                                                                                  #  TASK WHEN LOCK-ON IS ACHIEVED.
026797,004575: 
026798,004576: 32,2545                                           BANK     32                                    
026799,004577: 32,2000                                           SETLOC   F2DPS*32                              
026800,004578: 32,2000                                           BANK                                           
026801,004579: 
026802,004580: 32,2545                                           COUNT*   $$/R29                                
026803,004581: 32,2545  E3,1760                                  EBANK=   LOSVDT/4                              
026804,004582: 
026805,004583: 32,2545           34753        R29DODES           CA       ONE                                   
026806,004584: 32,2546           55107                           TS       TANG                                  #  INDICATE 1ST PASS THRU VECTOR LOOP.
026807,004585: 32,2547           34756                           CA       FIVE                                  
026808,004586: 
026809,004587: 32,2550           10000        R29DVBEG           CCS      A                                     #  COUNT DOWN BY TWOS IN VECTOR LOOP.
026810,004588: 32,2551           54002                           TS       Q                                     
026811,004589: 32,2552           11107                           CCS      TANG                                  
026812,004590: 32,2553           12561                           TCF      R29DPAS1                              #  DO THIS ON 1ST PASS THRU LOOP.
026813,004591: 
026814,004592: 32,2554           00006                           EXTEND                                         #  (A "PASS" HERE MEANS 3 TIMES AROUND).
026815,004593: 32,2555           50002                           INDEX    Q                                     
026816,004594: 32,2556           31761                           DCA      LOSVDT/4                              
026817,004595: 32,2557           50002                           INDEX    Q                                     
026818,004596: 32,2560           21102                           DAS      LOSSM                                 #  ADVANCE LOS VECTOR 1/2 SECOND.
026819,004597: 
026820,004598: 32,2561           00006        R29DPAS1           EXTEND                                         
026821,004599: 32,2562           50002                           INDEX    Q                                     
026822,004600: 32,2563           31102                           DCA      LOSSM                                 
026823,004601: 32,2564           50002                           INDEX    Q                                     #  MOVE CURRENT LOS (1ST PASS) OR LOS PRO-
026824,004602: 32,2565           52156                           DXCH     MPAC       +1                         #  JECTED 1/2 SEC AHEAD (2ND PASS).
026825,004603: 32,2566           11107                           CCS      TANG                                  
026826,004604: 32,2567           12575                           TCF      R29DVEND                              #  BUG OUT HERE IN 1ST PASS.
026827,004605: 
026828,004606: 32,2570           00006                           EXTEND                                         
026829,004607: 32,2571           50002                           INDEX    Q                                     
026830,004608: 32,2572           31761                           DCA      LOSVDT/4                              
026831,004609: 32,2573           50002                           INDEX    Q                                     
026832,004610: 32,2574           20156                           DAS      MPAC       +1                         #  PROJECT LOS 1 SECOND AHEAD (2ND PASS).
026833,004611: 
026834,004612: 32,2575           10002        R29DVEND           CCS      Q                                     
026835,004613: 32,2576           12550                           TCF      R29DVBEG                              #  BRANCH TO CONTINUE VECTOR LOOP.
026836,004614:

Page 612 

026838,004616:                                                                                                  #  UNITIZE AND TRANSFORM TO NAV BASE AXES THE PRESENT LOS (1ST PASS) OR THE 1-SEC PROJECTED LOS (2ND PASS).
026839,004617: 
026840,004618: 32,2577           52156                           DXCH     MPAC       +1                         
026841,004619: 32,2600           52155                           DXCH     MPAC                                  
026842,004620: 32,2601           32770                           CA       R29FXLOC                              #  = ADRES INTB15+ -34D

026845,004623: 32,2604           01023                           CADR     UNIT                                  #  SQUARED, BORROW UNITIZING ROUTINE.
026846,004624: 32,2605           07531                           TC       MPACVBUF                              #  MOVE UNIT(LOS) TO AX*SR*T ARG AREA.
026847,004625: 
026848,004626: 32,2606           11107                           CCS      TANG                                  
026849,004627: 32,2607           12611                           TCF      +2
